-000024b0: 2f70 3e0a 3c70 3e54 6869 7320 6d6f 6475  /p>.<p>This modu
-000024c0: 6c65 2065 7874 656e 6473 204f 646f 6f20  le extends Odoo 
-000024d0: 6675 6e63 7469 6f6e 616c 6974 792c 2061  functionality, a
-000024e0: 6c6c 6f77 696e 6720 7573 6572 2074 6f20  llowing user to 
-000024f0: 6765 6e65 7261 7465 2062 6172 636f 6465  generate barcode
-00002500: 0a64 6570 656e 6469 6e67 206f 6e20 6120  .depending on a 
-00002510: 6769 7665 6e20 6261 7263 6f64 6520 7275  given barcode ru
-00002520: 6c65 2066 6f72 2061 6e79 204d 6f64 656c  le for any Model
-00002530: 2e3c 2f70 3e0a 3c70 3e46 6f72 2065 7861  .</p>.<p>For exa
-00002540: 6d70 6c65 2c20 6966 2074 6865 2062 6172  mple, if the bar
-00002550: 636f 6465 2070 6174 7465 726e 2069 7320  code pattern is 
-00002560: e280 9c32 30e2 80a6 2e2e 7b4e 4e4e 4444  ...20.....{NNNDD
-00002570: 7de2 809d 3a3c 2f70 3e0a 3c75 6c20 636c  }...:</p>.<ul cl
-00002580: 6173 733d 2273 696d 706c 6522 3e0a 3c6c  ass="simple">.<l
-00002590: 693e 7468 6520 4541 4e31 3320 636f 6465  i>the EAN13 code
-000025a0: 2077 696c 6c20 6265 6769 6e20 7769 7468   will begin with
-000025b0: 20e2 8098 3230 e280 992c 3c2f 6c69 3e0a   ...20...,</li>.
-000025c0: 3c6c 693e 666f 6c6c 6f77 6564 2062 7920  <li>followed by 
-000025d0: 3520 6469 6769 7473 2028 6e61 6d65 6420  5 digits (named 
-000025e0: 3c65 6d3e 4261 7263 6f64 6520 4261 7365  <em>Barcode Base
-000025f0: 3c2f 656d 3e20 696e 2074 6869 7320 6d6f  </em> in this mo
-00002600: 6475 6c65 292c 3c2f 6c69 3e0a 3c6c 693e  dule),</li>.<li>
-00002610: 666f 6c6c 6f77 6564 2062 7920 3520 6f74  followed by 5 ot
-00002620: 6865 7273 2064 6967 6974 7320 746f 2064  hers digits to d
-00002630: 6566 696e 6520 7468 6520 7661 7269 6162  efine the variab
-00002640: 6c65 2070 7269 6365 2077 6974 6820 3220  le price with 2 
-00002650: 6465 6369 6d61 6c73 2c3c 2f6c 693e 0a3c  decimals,</li>.<
-00002660: 6c69 3e74 6865 206c 6173 7420 6469 6769  li>the last digi
-00002670: 7420 2874 6865 2031 3372 6420 6469 6769  t (the 13rd digi
-00002680: 7429 2069 7320 7468 6520 636f 6e74 726f  t) is the contro
-00002690: 6c20 6469 6769 7420 2869 2e65 2e20 7468  l digit (i.e. th
-000026a0: 6520 6368 6563 6b73 756d 292e 3c2f 6c69  e checksum).</li
-000026b0: 3e0a 3c2f 756c 3e0a 3c70 3e57 6974 6820  >.</ul>.<p>With 
-000026c0: 7468 6973 206d 6f64 756c 652c 2069 7420  this module, it 
-000026d0: 6973 2070 6f73 7369 626c 6520 746f 3a3c  is possible to:<
-000026e0: 2f70 3e0a 3c75 6c20 636c 6173 733d 2273  /p>.<ul class="s
-000026f0: 696d 706c 6522 3e0a 3c6c 693e 4166 6665  imple">.<li>Affe
-00002700: 6374 2061 2070 6174 7465 726e 2028 6261  ct a pattern (ba
-00002710: 7263 6f64 652e 7275 6c65 2920 746f 2061  rcode.rule) to a
-00002720: 206d 6f64 656c 3c2f 6c69 3e0a 3c6c 693e   model</li>.<li>
-00002730: 3c64 6c20 636c 6173 733d 2266 6972 7374  <dl class="first

+00003810: 0a3c 703e 416c 7465 726e 6174 6976 656c  .<p>Alternativel
+00003820: 792c 2079 6f75 2063 616e 2064 6576 656c  y, you can devel

+00003920: 2f70 3e0a 3c70 7265 2063 6c61 7373 3d22  /p>.<pre class="
